});\n   165‚Üí    \n   166‚Üí    try {\n   167‚Üí      const aiModule = await import('@/lib/ai-stage-runner');\n   168‚Üí      const loadTime = Date.now() - startTime;\n   169‚Üí      \n   170‚Üí    \n   187‚Üí      console.log('[WizardShell] ‚úÖ AI stage runner function validated successfully');\n   188‚Üí      \n   189‚Üí    } catch (error: any) {\n   190‚Üí      const loadTime = Date.now() - startTime;\n   191‚Üí      const errorDetails = {\n   192‚Üí        loadTimeMs: loadTime,\n   193‚Üí        attempt: retryAttempt + 1,\n   194‚Üí        errorMessage: error.message,\n   195‚Üí \n   204‚Üí      console.error('[WizardShell] ‚ùå Failed to load AI stage runner:', errorDetails);\n   205‚Üí      \n   206‚Üí      setAiLoadAttempts(retryAttempt + 1);\n   207‚Üí    } else {\n   220‚Üí        // Final failure - show comprehensive error toast\n   221‚Üí        const comprehensiveError = `AI Module Load Failed After ${retryAttempt + 1} Attempts\n   222‚Üí\n     }}\n   255‚Üí              size=\"sm\"\n   256‚Üí            >\n   257‚Üí              Retry\n   258‚Üí            </Button>\n   259‚Üí          )\n   260‚Üí        });\n   261‚Üí      }\n 321‚Üí\n   322‚Üí    if (needsImmediateSave) {\n   323‚Üí      // Next tick save so React state has committed\n   324‚Üí      setTimeout(() => {\n   325‚Üí        saveDocument();\n   326‚Üí      }, (currentStageStates: Record<string, StageState>, stages: Stage[]): Record<string, StageState> => {\n   332‚Üí    const newStageStates = { ...currentStageStates };\n   333‚Üí    let changed = false;\n   334‚Üí\n   335‚Üí    stages.forEach(stage => {\n   336‚Üí      const currentState = newStageStates[stage.id];\n   337‚Üí      if (!currentState) return; // Should not happen if initialized depsMet = stage.dependencies.every(depId => \n   343‚Üí          newStageStates[depId]?.status === 'completed'\n   344‚Üí        );\n   345‚Üí      }\n   346‚Üí\n   347‚Üí      // Evaluate autorun conditions (more complex dependency logic)\n   348‚Üí      let autoRunConditionsMet = true;\n   349‚Üí      if (stage.autoRunConditions) {\n   350‚Üí        if (stage.autoRunConditions.requiresAll) {\n   351‚Üí          autoRunConditionsMet = stage.autoRunConditions.requiresAll.every(depId => \n   352‚Üí            newStageStates[depId]?.status === 'completed'\n   353‚Üí          );\n   354‚Üí        }\n   355‚Üí        if (autoRunConditionsMet && stage.autoRunConditions.requiresAny) {\n   356‚Üí          autoRunConditionsMet = stage.autoRunConditions.requiresAny.some(depId => \n   357‚Üí            newStageStates[depId]?.status === 'completed'\n   358‚Üí          );\n   359‚Üí        }\n   360‚Üí      }\n   361‚Üí      \n   362‚Üí      let isStale = false;\n   363‚Üí      if = new Date(currentState.completedAt).getTime();\n   366‚Üí        \n   367‚Üí        // Check staleness based on basic dependencies\n   368‚Üí        if (stage.dependencies && stage.dependencies.length > 0) {\n   369‚Üí          isStale = stage.dependencies.some(depId => {\n   370‚Üí            const depCompletedAt = newStageStates[depId]?.completedAt ? new Date(newStageStates[depId].completedAt).getTime() : 0;\n   371‚Üí            return depCompletedAt > stageCompletedAt || newStageStates[depId]?.isStale === true;\n   372‚Üí          });\n   373‚Üí        }\n   374‚Üí        \n   375‚Üí        // Also check staleness based on autorun conditions\n   376‚Üí        if (!isStale && stage.autoRunConditions?.requiresAll) {\n   377‚Üí          isStale = stage.autoRunConditions.requiresAll.some(depId => {\n   378‚Üí            const depCompletedAt = newStageStates[depId]?.completedAt ? new Date(newStageStates[depId].completedAt).getTime() : 0;\n   379‚Üí            return depCompletedAt > stageCompletedAt || newStageStates[depId]?.isStale === true;\n   380‚Üí          });\n   381‚Üí        }\n   382‚Üí        \n   383‚Üí        // Also check staleness based on autorun dependencies\n   384‚Üí        if (!isStale && stage.autorunDependsOn && stage.autorunDependsOn.length > 0) {\n   385‚Üí          isStale = stage.autorunDependsOn.some(depId => {\n   386‚Üí            const depCompletedAt = newStageStates[depId]?.completedAt ? new Date(newStageStates[depId].completedAt).getTime() : 0;\n   387‚Üí            return depCompletedAt > stageCompletedAt || newStageStates[depId]?.isStale === true;\n   388‚Üí          });\n   389‚Üí        }\n   390‚Üí      }\n   391‚Üí\n   392‚Üí      // Evaluate autorun dependencies (separate from activation dependencies)\n   393‚Üí      let autorunDepsMet = true;\n   394‚Üí      if (stage.autorunDependsOn && stage.autorunDependsOn.length > 0) {\n   395‚Üí        // Use explicit autorun dependencies\n   396‚Üí        autorunDepsMet = stage.autorunDependsOn.every(depId => \n   397‚Üí          newStageStates[depId]?.status === 'completed'\n   398‚Üí        );\n   399‚Üí      } else {\n   400‚Üí        // Fall back to regular dependencies (backward compatibility)\n   401‚Üí        autorunDepsMet = depsMet;\n   402‚Üí      }\n   403‚Üí\n   404‚Üí      // Determine if stage should auto-run\n   405‚Üí      let shouldAutoRun = false;\n   406‚Üí      if (stage.autoRun && currentState.status === 'idle' && !currentState.isEditingOutput) {\n   407‚Üí        if (stage.autoRunConditions) {\n   408‚Üí          // Use complex autorun conditions AND autorun dependencies\n   409‚Üí          shouldAutoRun = depsMet && autoRunConditionsMet && autorunDepsMet;\n   410‚Üí        } else {\n   411‚Üí          // Use simple dependency logic - stage must be active (depsMet) AND autorun deps met\n   412‚Üí          shouldAutoRun = depsMet && autorunDepsMet;\n   413‚Üí        }\n   414‚Üí      }\n   415‚Üí\n   416‚Üí      if (\n   417‚Üí        currentState.depsAreMet !== depsMet ||\n   418‚Üí        currentState.isStale !== isStale ||\n   419‚Üí        currentState.shouldAutoRun !== shouldAutoRun\n   420‚Üí      ) {\n   421‚Üí        newStageStates[stage.id] = {\n   422‚Üí          ...currentState,\n   423‚Üí          depsAreMet: depsMet,\n   424‚Üí Return original if no change to avoid re-render\n   433‚Üí  };\n   434‚Üí  \n   435‚Üí  // Effect for initial and subsequent dependency evaluations\n   436‚Üí  useEffect(() => {\n   437‚Üí 441‚Üí  }, []); // Runs once on mount, subsequent calls via updateStageState\n   442‚Üí\n   443‚Üí\n   444‚Üí  useEffect(() => {\n   445‚Üí    instance.workflow.stages.forEach(stage => {\n   446‚Üí }, [instance.stageStates, instance.workflow.stages]); \n   455‚Üí\n   456‚Üí\n   457‚Üí  useEffect(() => {\n   458‚Üí    const titleStageId = instance.workflow.config?.setTitleFromStageOutput;\n   459‚Üí    if (titleStageId) {\n   460‚Üí      const titleStageState = instance.stageStates[titleStageId];\n   461‚Üí      if (titleStageState?.status === 'completed' && titleStageState.output) {\n 495‚Üí\n   496‚Üí\n   497‚Üí  const handleInputChange = (stageId: string, fieldName: string, value: any) => {\n   498‚Üí    // This is primarily for simple input types like 'textarea' or 'context' userInput: data, \n   525‚Üí        status: 'idle',\n   526‚Üí        isStale: true\n   527‚Üí      });\n   528‚Üí    }\n   529‚Üí  };\n   530‚Üí\n   531‚Üí  const handleRunStage = useCallback(async Franz AI Writer - Storybook Component Library\n\nThis directory contains the Storybook configuration for the Franz AI Writer Next.js application, providing comprehensive component documentation and interactive development environment.\n\n## Overview\n\nStorybook serves as our component library documentation system, allowing developers to:\n- View and interact with UI components in isolation\n- Test different component states and props\n- Access comprehensive documentation and usage examples\n- Develop components independently from the main application\n\n## Setup and Installation\n\n### Prerequisites\n- Node.js 18+ and npm\n- Franz AI Writer project dependencies installed\n\n### Installation\n```bash\n# Install dependencies (if not already installed)\nnpm install\n\n# Start Storybook development server\nnpm run storybook\n```\n\nThe Storybook dev server will start at `http://localhost:6006`.\n\n### Build Production Version\n```bash\n# Build static Storybook for deployment\nnpm run build-storybook\n\n# Serve built Storybook locally\nnpm run storybook:serve\n```\n\n## Configuration\n\n### Main Configuration (`main.ts`)\n- **Framework**: Next.js with TypeScript support\n- **Story Discovery**: Automatically finds `*.stories.tsx` files in `src/`\n- **Addons**: Essential Storybook addons for controls, documentation, and interactions\n- **TypeScript**: Configured with react-docgen-typescript for automatic prop documentation\n- **Features**: Experimental RSC support for React Server Components\n\n### Preview Configuration (`preview.ts`)\n- **Global Styles**: Imports the application's global CSS (Tailwind CSS)\n- **Controls**: Automatic control generation for colors and dates\n- **Viewport**: Responsive breakpoints matching the design system\n- **Documentation**: Table of contents enabled for comprehensive docs\n\n## Architecture\n\n### Design System Integration\n- **Tailwind CSS**: Full integration with the project's design system\n- **Shadcn/UI**: All shadcn/ui components are documented with variants\n- **Blue-based Theme**: Consistent with the application's color scheme\n- **Space Grotesk**: Typography matches the application's font choices\n\n### Component Coverage\n- **UI Components**: Button, Card, Badge, and other foundational components\n- **Wizard Components**: Stage cards, wizard shell, and workflow-specific components\n- **Layout Components**: Header, footer, navigation components\n- **Interactive Examples**: Real-world usage patterns and compositions\n\n## Story Organization\n\n### Naming Convention\nStories follow the pattern: `ComponentName.stories.tsx`\n\n### Categories\n- **UI Components** (`src/components/ui/`)\n- **Wizard Components** (`src/components/wizard/`)\n- **Layout Components** (`src/components/layout/`)\n\n### Story Structure\nEach story file includes:\n- **Default export**: Component metadata and configuration\n- **Multiple stories**: Different states, variants, and use cases\n- **Controls**: Interactive props for testing\n- **Documentation**: Usage examples and guidelines\n\n## Development Workflow\n\n### Creating New Stories\n1. Create a `ComponentName.stories.tsx` file alongside your component\n2. Define the default export with component metadata\n3. Create individual stories for different states/variants\n4. Add controls for interactive testing\n5. Include documentation and usage examples\n\n### Best Practices\n- **Isolation**: Stories should not depend on external application state\n- **Documentation**: Include comprehensive prop documentation\n- **Accessibility**: Test components with different accessibility settings\n- **Responsive**: Test components across different viewport sizes\n- **Real Data**: Use realistic mock data in stories\n\n## Component Documentation\n\n### JSDoc Integration\n- All components include comprehensive JSDoc comments\n- Prop descriptions are automatically extracted\n- Usage examples and best practices are documented\n- Type information is preserved and displayed\n\n### Interactive Controls\n- **Automatic Controls**: Generated from TypeScript prop types\n- **Custom Controls**: Manually configured for complex props\n- **Validation**: Real-time validation of prop values\n- **Presets**: Common configurations for quick testing\n\n## Usage Examples\n\n### Basic Component Story\n```typescript\nimport type { Meta, StoryObj } from '@storybook/react';\nimport { Button } from './button';\n\nconst meta: Meta<typeof Button> = {\n  title: 'UI/Button',\n  component: Button,\n  parameters: {\n    layout: 'centered',\n  },\n  tags: ['autodocs'],\n};\n\nexport default meta;\ntype Story = StoryObj<typeof meta>;\n\nexport const Default: Story = {\n  args: {\n    children: 'Button',\n  },\n};\n```\n\n### Complex Component with Controls\n```typescript\nexport const AllVariants: Story = {\n  render: () => (\n    <div className=\"flex gap-4\">\n      <Button variant=\"default\">Default</Button>\n      <Button variant=\"secondary\">Secondary</Button>\n      <Button variant=\"outline\">Outline</Button>\n      <Button variant=\"ghost\">Ghost</Button>\n    </div>\n  ),\n};\n```\n\n## Integration with Development\n\n### Hot Reloading\n- Changes to components are automatically reflected in Storybook\n- Stories themselves support hot reloading\n- Global styles and configuration updates are reflected immediately\n\n### TypeScript Support\n- Full TypeScript support with type checking\n- Automatic prop extraction from TypeScript interfaces\n- IntelliSense support in story files\n\n## Troubleshooting\n\n### Common Issues\n\n1. **Import Errors**: Ensure all dependencies are installed and paths are correct\n2. **Style Issues**: Check that
